**Plugin Process Supervisor** (pkg/plugins/manager/process/): The `Service` struct in process.go implements the Manager interface, providing `Start()` and `Stop()` methods to manage the lifecycle of backend plugin processes. The `startPluginAndKeepItAlive()` method initiates a plugin and spawns a goroutine running the `keepPluginAlive()` method.\\n\\n2. **Plugin Restart Policy on Crash** (pkg/plugins/manager/process/process.go): The `keepPluginAlive()` method implements the restart mechanism. It uses a ticker that checks every second if a plugin process has exited using `p.Exited()`. If the process has exited unexpectedly, it automatically restarts the plugin using `p.Start(context.Background())`. This provides automatic recovery from crashes for managed plugins (non-core plugins).\\n\\n3. **gRPC Client Connection** (pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/): The `grpcPlugin` struct in grpc_plugin.go manages the gRPC connection to external backend plugins. The `Start()` method creates a new `plugin.Client` using `newClientConfig()` from client.go, which sets up the gRPC communication. The `getPluginClient()` method retrieves the active ClientV2 and checks if the connection is valid. Connection configuration handles both standard process mode and container mode for plugin execution.\\n\\n4. **gRPC Plugin Connection Setup** (pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/client.go): The `newClientConfig()` function creates the gRPC client configuration with proper handshake settings and plugin negotiation. The `PluginDescriptor` struct encapsulates plugin configuration including executable path, arguments, and environment variables.\\n\\n5. **Plugin Health Check Implementation** (pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/client_v2.go): The `ClientV2.CheckHealth()` method sends health check requests to the plugin via gRPC. They are not managed (process-wise) but still provide CheckHealth and other backend operations by delegating to their handlers.\\n\\n9. **Client Service** (pkg/plugins/manager/client/client.go): The `Service` implements the client interface, handling CheckHealth requests by retrieving the appropriate plugin from the registry and delegating to its CheckHealth method with error handling for unavailable plugins and method not implemented scenarios.\\n\\nThe architecture ensures that managed external backend plugins are automatically restarted when they crash, their health is continuously monitored, and gRPC connections are properly established and maintained.\"\n}\nEOF\ncat answer.json\n","description":"Create the answer.json file with findings"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":9,"cache_creation_input_tokens":235,"cache_read_input_tokens":62402,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":235},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"fbaffb09-4888-41d5-b651-a04975adbce8","uuid":"295b8a1e-5a3b-44e5-9079-b1e1329d3c20"}

The `startPluginAndKeepItAlive()` method initiates a plugin and spawns a goroutine running the `keepPluginAlive()` method.\\n\\n2. **Plugin Restart Policy on Crash** (pkg/plugins/manager/process/process.go): The `keepPluginAlive()` method implements the restart mechanism. It uses a ticker that checks every second if a plugin process has exited using `p.Exited()`. If the process has exited unexpectedly, it automatically restarts the plugin using `p.Start(context.Background())`. This provides automatic recovery from crashes for managed plugins (non-core plugins).\\n\\n3. **gRPC Client Connection** (pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/): The `grpcPlugin` struct in grpc_plugin.go manages the gRPC connection to external backend plugins. The `Start()` method creates a new `plugin.Client` using `newClientConfig()` from client.go, which sets up the gRPC communication. The `getPluginClient()` method retrieves the active ClientV2 and checks if the connection is valid. Connection configuration handles both standard process mode and container mode for plugin execution.\\n\\n4. **gRPC Plugin Connection Setup** (pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/client.go): The `newClientConfig()` function creates the gRPC client configuration with proper handshake settings and plugin negotiation. The `containerClientConfig()` function provides container-based plugin execution when enabled. The `PluginDescriptor` struct encapsulates plugin configuration including executable path, arguments, and environment variables.\\n\\n5. **Plugin Health Check Implementation** (pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/client_v2.go): The `ClientV2.CheckHealth()` method sends health check requests to the plugin via gRPC. It dispatches to the DiagnosticsClient and handles various error conditions including Unimplemented status (returns Unknown health status). The method is called from both the gRPC plugin wrapper (grpc_plugin.go line 183-189) and the plugin client service (manager/client/client.go).\\n\\n6. **Plugin Interface and Lifecycle** (pkg/plugins/backendplugin/ifaces.go): Defines the `Plugin` interface that all backend plugins must implement, including Start(), Stop(), IsManaged(), Exited(), Decommission(), IsDecommissioned(), Target(), and handlers for CheckHealth, QueryData, CallResource, and other backend operations.\\n\\n7. **Plugin Wrapper** (pkg/plugins/plugins.go): The main `Plugin` struct wraps the backend plugin client and delegates lifecycle methods (Start, Stop, Exited, CheckHealth) to the underlying backend plugin implementation.\\n\\n8. **Core Plugin Support** (pkg/plugins/backendplugin/coreplugin/core_plugin.go): Core (built-in) plugins implement the same Plugin interface through the `corePlugin` struct. They are not managed (process-wise) but still provide CheckHealth and other backend operations by delegating to their handlers.\\n\\n9. **Client Service** (pkg/plugins/manager/client/client.go): The `Service` implements the client interface, handling CheckHealth requests by retrieving the appropriate plugin from the registry and delegating to its CheckHealth method with error handling for unavailable plugins and method not implemented scenarios.\\n\\nThe architecture ensures that managed external backend plugins are automatically restarted when they crash, their health is continuously monitored, and gRPC connections are properly established and maintained.\"\n}","stderr":"","interrupted":false,"isImage":false,"noOutputExpected":false}}
